e > bestScore) {\n   125\t      bestScore = score;\n   126\t      bestTarget = t
arget;\n   127\t    }\n   128\t  }\n   129\t  \n   130\t  if (isErrorRelated &&

 133\t  }\n   134\t  \n   135\t  if (isIssue && bestScore < 4) {\n   136\t    re
turn {\n   137\t      target: \'.issues/\',\n   138\t      isIssue: true,\n   13
9\t      priority: issuePriority,\n   140\t      reason: \'檢測到任務關鍵字（要
做/跟進/任務）\',\n   141\t      confidence: \'high\'\n   142\t    };\n   143\t 
}\n   144\t  \n   145\t  if (bestTarget && bestScore > 0) {\n   146\t    return 
{\n   147\t      target: bestTarget,\n   148\t      isIssue: false,\n   149\t   
  reason: reasons[bestTarget][0] || \'內容匹配\',\n   150\t      confidence: bes
tScore >= 3 ? \'high\' : bestScore >= 2 ? \'medium\' : \'low\'\n   151\t    };\n
  152\t  }\n   153\t  \n   154\t  return {\n   155\t    target: \'MEMORY.md\',\n
  156\t    isIssue: false,\n   157\t    reason: \'默認分類（一般記憶）\',\n   15

341\t}\n   342\t\n   343\t// Level 3: Preference Learning\n   344\tfunction chec
kAndPromoteToPreference(text, state) {\n   345\t  const threeMonthsAgo = new Dat
e();\n   346\t  threeMonthsAgo.setMonth(threeMonthsAgo.getMonth() - 3);\n   347\
t  \n   348\t  // Extract core content (remove "記住", "記得" etc.)\n   349\t  c
onst coreContent = extractCoreContent(text);\n   350\t  \n   351\t  // Count occ
urrences in last 3 months\n   352\t  let count = 0;\n   353\t  const occurrences
= [];\n   354\t  \n   355\t  for (const item of state.processedItems || []) {\n 
 356\t    const itemTime = new Date(item.time);\n   357\t    if (itemTime >= thr
eeMonthsAgo) {\n   358\t      const itemCore = extractCoreContent(item.fullText 
|| item.text);\n   359\t      if (isContentSimilar(coreContent, itemCore)) {\n  
360\t        count++;\n   361\t        occurrences.push({ time: item.time, text:
item.fullText || item.text });\n   362\t      }\n   363\t    }\n   364\t  }\n   
365\t  \n   366\t  // If 3+ occurrences, promote to P0 preference\n   367\t  if 
(count >= 3) {\n   368\t    const preference = {\n   369\t      id: `pref-${Date
.now()}`,\n   370\t      content: coreContent,\n   371\t      fullText: text.sub
string(0, 200),\n   372\t      count,\n   373\t      firstSeen: occurrences[0]?.
time,\n   374\t      lastSeen: occurrences[occurrences.length - 1]?.time,\n   37
5\t      promotedDate: getHKTDateTime(),\n   376\t      status: \'auto_promoted\
'\n   377\t    };\n   378\t    \n   379\t    // Check if already promoted\n   38
0\t    state.preferences = state.preferences || [];\n   381\t    const alreadyPr
omoted = state.preferences.some(p => \n   382\t      isContentSimilar(extractCor
eContent(p.content), coreContent)\n   383\t    );\n   384\t    \n   385\t    if 
(!alreadyPromoted) {\n   386\t      state.preferences.push(preference);\n   387\
t      log(`🎯 Level 3: Auto-promoted to P0 preference after ${count} occurrence
s`);\n   388\t      log(`   Content: "${coreContent.substring(0, 60)}..."`);\n  
389\t      \n   390\t      // Optionally notify user\n   391\t      notifyPrefer
encePromotion(preference);\n   392\t    }\n   393\t  }\n   394\t}\n   395\t\n   
396\tfunction extractCoreContent(text) {\n   397\t  // Remove common prefixes\n 
 398\t  return text\n   399\t    .replace(/記住|記得|唔好忘記|記低|請記住/gi, \'
\')\n   400\t    .replace(/規則係[:：]/gi, \'\')\n   401\t    .replace(/^\\s+/, 
\'\')\n   402\t    .substring(0, 100)\n   403\t    .toLowerCase();\n   404\t}\n 
 405\t\n   406\tfunction isContentSimilar(a, b) {\n   407\t  // Simple similarit
y: check if first 50 chars match or 70% overlap\n   408\t  if (a.length < 10 || 
b.length < 10) return false;\n   409\t  \n   410\t  const aStart = a.substring(0
, 50);\n   411\t  const bStart = b.substring(0, 50);\n   412\t  \n   413\t  if (
aStart === bStart) return true;\n   414\t  \n   415\t  // Check word overlap\n  
416\t  const aWords = a.split(/\\s+/);\n   417\t  const bWords = b.split(/\\s+/)
;\n   418\t  const commonWords = aWords.filter(w => bWords.includes(w));\n   419
\t  const similarity = commonWords.length / Math.max(aWords.length, bWords.lengt
h);\n   420\t  \n   421\t  return similarity >= 0.7;\n   422\t}\n   423\t\n   42

y this preference in future without asking.`;\n   427\t    \n   428\t    // Sani

age.replace(/"/g, \'\\\\"\').replace(/\\n/g, \' \').substring(0, 1800);\n   430\

  466\t    // Build header row\n   467\t    const header = columns.map(c => c.he
ader).join(\' | \');\n   468\t\n   469\t    // Build separator row with alignmen
t\n   470\t    const separator = columns.map(c => {\n   471\t      const align =
c.align || \'left\';\n   472\t      if (align === \'center\') return \':---:\';\
n   473\t      if (align === \'right\') return \'---:\';\n   474\t      return \
'---\';  // left align (default)\n   475\t    }).join(\' | \');\n   476\t\n   47
7\t    // Build data rows\n   478\t    const rows = data.map(item =>\n   479\t  
   columns.map(c => {\n   480\t        const value = item[c.key];\n   481\t     
  // Handle null/undefined\n   482\t        if (value === null || value === unde
fined) return \'\';\n   483\t        // Convert to string and escape pipe charac
ters\n   484\t        return String(value).replace(/\\|/g, \'\\\\|\');\n   485\t
     }).join(\' | \')\n   486\t    );\n   487\t\n   488\t    return [header, sep
arator, ...rows].join(\'\\n\');\n   489\t  }\n   490\t}\n   491\t\n   492\t// ==
